  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081811384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2872203195010936718"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: SPOILER-FREE ::: </b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420494120i/13232085.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>WOW!! What an amazing, unique story!!</b><br/><br/><i>Never Never</i> was fast-paced, thrilling, mysterious, exciting, romantic, and kept me guessing the whole way though. I literally could not put it down and I can't wait for the next book in this fantastic new series!!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Best friends since they could walk.<br/>In love since the age of fourteen.<br/>Complete strangers since this morning.<br/><br/>He'll do anything to remember.<br/>She'll do anything to forget.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>This is the first book</span>
  <span id="freeText2872203195010936718" style="display:none"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: SPOILER-FREE ::: </b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420494120i/13232085.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>WOW!! What an amazing, unique story!!</b><br><br><i>Never Never</i> was fast-paced, thrilling, mysterious, exciting, romantic, and kept me guessing the whole way though. I literally could not put it down and I can't wait for the next book in this fantastic new series!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Best friends since they could walk.<br>In love since the age of fourteen.<br>Complete strangers since this morning.<br><br>He'll do anything to remember.<br>She'll do anything to forget.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>This is the first book of a series co-written by Colleen Hoover and Tarryn Fisher. Colleen wrote the guy's POV, Tarryn wrote the girl's, and the two halves of the story were blended together seamlessly.<br><br>This is going to be a shorter review because my honest opinion is that it's best to go into this book knowing as little as possible about the actual story so I won't tell you anything that'll ruin the experience here. But I can say that I was hooked from the very first page and completely drawn into these characters' lives.<br><br>The only things I knew before starting it other than what the blurb said was that it was a real-world story (somewhere between YA and NA) with a very slight paranormal twist to it. Just to clarify that a little: there are no vampires or ghosts or any such beings, it's more just in the background in a subtle, undefined, but enthralling way. But I don't want to say more though because I want you to let it unfold as you read.<br><br>Dozens of theories about what could be happening to these characters were constantly playing in my head as I flew through the pages, and then just when I began to think I had an idea where the story was going, a surprising new layer to the mystery was revealed that sent full body chills running through me!!<br><br>The ending was a bit of a cliffhanger, but it was a very exciting one (not an oh-crap-why?! one). It was a very logical stopping point but it also spun the story in a crazy cool new direction that opened up such thrilling possibilities for the next book! Really, truly... don't wait to start this series -- just dive right in!<br><br>There's a reason we've come to love Colleen and Tarryn's writing. They've earned our trust and fully deserve it. With <i>Never Never</i> , they delivered a suspenseful, captivating, heart-pounding page turner with a love story at it's core. I'm absolutely addicted to this series and can't wait to see what happens next!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m gonna make you fall in love with me again.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><i>SEQUEL RELEASE DATE: MAY 17, 2015</i><br>_______________________________________<br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/subscribe/" rel="nofollow noopener">Subscribe by email</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<div id="review_1166258553" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1166258553" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1166258553?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1166258553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11682643563584760562"> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421141376i/13328289._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='370' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Surprise, surprise, this is my first time giving a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover' title='Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Colleen Hoover</a> book one star as a rating. Actually, I have never never (HA!) rated one of her works less than three stars. Her novels are usually enjoyable, but I very much disliked this one…and am not going to feel sorry about it. There are some books on Goodreads that you can feel uncomfortable writing a negative review for because of how many of your friends loved it or people in general, but I’m not going to let this one be one of them. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24378015.Never_Never__Never_Never___1_' title='Never Never (Never Never, #1) by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Nev</a></span>
  <span id="freeText11682643563584760562" style="display:none"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421141376i/13328289._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="370" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Surprise, surprise, this is my first time giving a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" title="Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a> book one star as a rating. Actually, I have never never (HA!) rated one of her works less than three stars. Her novels are usually enjoyable, but I very much disliked this one…and am not going to feel sorry about it. There are some books on Goodreads that you can feel uncomfortable writing a negative review for because of how many of your friends loved it or people in general, but I’m not going to let this one be one of them. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24378015.Never_Never__Never_Never___1_" title="Never Never (Never Never, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Never Never</a>, you <s>sucked</s> missed the mark. So badly. <br><br>First off, this is not New Adult; it’s <b>Young Adult</b>. The characters are in a freaking high school! And there is freaking high school boy drama! Secondly, this is not a story; it’s a BIG and FRUSTRATING teaser. If we had an entire novel, what I just read would have been the first two chapters of it. (Because I’m taking out the useless ones only meaning to confuse us more.) In fact, it is as if the authors told themselves ‘‘The more we confuse our readers and add unexplained information, the MORE they’re going to freak and LOVE IT!’’ Nuh-uh. Yes for the former: I am indeed freaking out at how much I disliked this but never in a million years would I come to love this short story (ugh, it even hurts to call it that.) <br><br>Alright, so you’re probably wondering about the characters now. Are they nice? Beautiful? Well-developped? <i>
  <b>‘‘I think my mother may be a bitch.’’</b>
</i> Yeah, that was Charlie, the main character, you just heard. She thinks her mom is a bitch because the latter wants to protect her against Silas whom <u>took her husband away from her</u> – I assume – and hurt Charlie. But are we given real detail on that? Well of course not, that would have been giving the readers too soon what they want. Why not let them linger a little while longer…until May 2015 perhaps? I hope this is at least a duology. Let’s not even start on Silas. The author pictured him as a guy hopelessly in love with Charlie (even before really knowing her) with so much intensity that I wasn’t convinced anymore. It was TOO MUCH. And TOO SOON.<br><br>There is cheating. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(It may not count for some, but that made me doubt Charlie and Silas’ true feelings for each other.) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>There are plenty of unanswered questions. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(How did they lose their memories? And why? Because they wanted to forget what they did to each other? Why did they do that in the FIRST place? What did Charlie’s dad do? – more detail please! What did the files contain?) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>There is a cliffhanger. <br><br>There is an insta-love vibe and a high paranormal one too. It’s a very unrealistic contemporary story with a hard to imagine and unbelievable romance and a deal of under-developed secondary characters. And the writing wasn’t even that good! Simplistic and sometimes in contradiction with the personality of the characters. Often in the book, Silas says how he doesn’t like what Charlie does with a voice that implies more ‘‘I dislike this chick.’’ than ‘‘I’m deeply in love with this beautiful girl.’’ <br><br>Also, this:<br><br><i>
  <b>I’m standing on the edge of the lawn, looking down his street when he walks up behind me. I don’t hear him approach, but I smell him. I don’t know how, since he smells like the outdoors.</b>
</i><br><br>This is ridiculous. Are you sure you didn’t <i>sense</i> him, instead? *shakes head*<br><br>I did not like this and would not even recommend it to my worst enemy. <u>I know many of you liked it though and I respect that.</u> I’m debating whether reading the sequel or not, because who would be okay with having so many unanswered questions on their minds? But I will not prioritize it even a tiny little bit.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11682643563584760562" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1167691271" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1167691271" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1167691271?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1167691271" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14846567940712437426">Update 2016: I'm not going to change my rating because I did enjoy this book, but I just want to issue a warning that I was so so disappointed with the ending of this series: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1284596696'>https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br/>...............................................................................................<br/><br/>I must say... even though I've had many issues with Hoover's books in the past, <b>she and Tarryn Fisher have weaved one hell of a compelling tale here.</b><br/><br/>The only real downside to this first inst</span>
  <span id="freeText14846567940712437426" style="display:none">Update 2016: I'm not going to change my rating because I did enjoy this book, but I just want to issue a warning that I was so so disappointed with the ending of this series: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1284596696">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br />...............................................................................................<br /><br />I must say... even though I've had many issues with Hoover's books in the past, <b>she and Tarryn Fisher have weaved one hell of a compelling tale here.</b><br /><br />The only real downside to this first installment is how quickly it was over, leaving us hanging with an evil cliffhanger that won't be resolved until May! This strange little book gives up so few of its secrets - a fact I might have withdrawn stars for if it wasn't such a damn intriguing pageturner.<br /><br />I'm going to be honest: Colleen Hoover has been responsible for many of my rants in the past and some might think me a masochist for even trying to enjoy another of her novels. I hated the way she glorified controlling boyfriends in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15717943.Hopeless__Hopeless___1_" title="Hopeless (Hopeless, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Hopeless</a>. I thought the writing in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13372690.Slammed__Slammed___1_" title="Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Slammed</a> showcased an author who had not yet found her footing. And <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17788403.Maybe_Someday__Maybe___1_" title="Maybe Someday (Maybe, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Maybe Someday</a> had more than its fair share of slut-shaming. <br /><br />But... I've said in my past (negative) reviews that I like Hoover's easy-to-digest style of writing that demands you turn the pages. I like how her characters are mostly three dimensional and not all typical NA stereotypes. So I cast aside my reservations and tumbled into this... mystery? Romance? Paranormal thriller? The jury's still out.<br /><br />This book opens with our two narrators having absolutely no memory of who they are, where they live, who their friends and family are... or how they managed to get in this state. Piecing together clues about their lives and their relationship, it seems like the more they discover the weirder everything gets. <b>Who were they before? How did they lose their memories? Do they even want to find out?</b><br /><br />Romance does come out when Charlie and Silas are trying to figure out the details of their relationship - as well as many skeletons in the closet - but unlike Hoover's other works, this story feels like so much more than a romance. <b>It's dark, mysterious, even creepy at times.</b> Probably not for readers who like a clear distinction between the realistic and the supernatural because I'm still not sure which applies here. <br /><br />Characters I care about, complex relationships (not just of the romantic kind), and a whopping great mystery... I'm ready for the sequel. Now please.<br /><br /><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://mycountryheart.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14846567940712437426" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15361977935450204170"><b>4 Mind-F*ck Stars.</b><br/>	<br/>I will not tell you much about this, because in this kind of books, the more blind you go in, the better. So let me tell you my reaction during pretty much the whole length of this book: <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420840721i/13276852._SY540_.png' width='350' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Charlie and Silas woke up one morning without remembering anything or anyone. The people around them know who they are, they have lives, they have family, that have friends… they just don’t remember absolutely anything. They start to try to figure out what happened to them… but they more they </span>
  <span id="freeText15361977935450204170" style="display:none"><b>4 Mind-F*ck Stars.</b><br>	<br>I will not tell you much about this, because in this kind of books, the more blind you go in, the better. So let me tell you my reaction during pretty much the whole length of this book: <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420840721i/13276852._SY540_.png" width="350" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Charlie and Silas woke up one morning without remembering anything or anyone. The people around them know who they are, they have lives, they have family, that have friends… they just don’t remember absolutely anything. They start to try to figure out what happened to them… but they more they dig, the more questions start to appear. <br>So get ready for a very strange and mysterious ride. You’re going to love it! <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412730041ra/11414792.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I first heard about a book written by Colleen and Tarryn together I thought: <i>“That has to be the stupidest idea ever.” </i><br>How can you put together the woman who wrote Slammed and the woman who wrote Mud Vain and expect it to work? <br>Well, I’m happy to say that I was completely mistaken: this book brought the best of both worlds. We have the dark and compelling mind-f*ck that Tarryn got us used to, but we also have the sweet, romantic and whimsical feeling Colleen always give us. <br>But this book left a lot of question unanswered… no, it left ALL the questions unanswered, so I really can’t wait for the next installment. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Meh. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Well, they technically cheated on each other in the past. But neither of them remember doing it or why. And they both become pretty despised with themselves when they find out.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Cliffhanger. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1081813145" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1081813145" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081813145?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081813145" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4880366020746423195"><br/><b>4 <i>Never stop. Never forget.</i> stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/97ea5ead-53fc-4b18-addf-df5c6191d730_zps18f01d56.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421229084i/13343582.jpg' alt=' photo 97ea5ead-53fc-4b18-addf-df5c6191d730_zps18f01d56.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Colleen Hoover. Tarryn Fisher. Two authors I love. Two distinctly different writing styles. Somehow, these two authors were able to collaborate and blend their styles together and <i>Never Never</i> was born. It’s one of those books that you finish and think... what the hell did I just read? Which didn’t surprise me. That’s happened with every Tarryn book I’ve read.<br/><br/>Charlie and Silas are in high school. Apparently they’re popular and they’re boyfriend and girlfriend</span>
  <span id="freeText4880366020746423195" style="display:none"><br><b>4 <i>Never stop. Never forget.</i> stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/97ea5ead-53fc-4b18-addf-df5c6191d730_zps18f01d56.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421229084i/13343582.jpg" alt=" photo 97ea5ead-53fc-4b18-addf-df5c6191d730_zps18f01d56.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Colleen Hoover. Tarryn Fisher. Two authors I love. Two distinctly different writing styles. Somehow, these two authors were able to collaborate and blend their styles together and <i>Never Never</i> was born. It’s one of those books that you finish and think... what the hell did I just read? Which didn’t surprise me. That’s happened with every Tarryn book I’ve read.<br><br>Charlie and Silas are in high school. Apparently they’re popular and they’re boyfriend and girlfriend. They also can’t remember a thing. Not about who they are, who their family and friends are, who each other are. Nothing. Forgetting is scary. Remembering may be as equally terrifying. All they know is that they are in this together. They are connected. They forgot together, now they’ll try to remember together. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/e3b7a5dd-b178-407e-a1b0-29dc990a7a8e_zpsd0dbfa33.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421229084i/13343583.jpg" alt=" photo e3b7a5dd-b178-407e-a1b0-29dc990a7a8e_zpsd0dbfa33.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>CoHo has done it again. Written a wonderfully swoonworthy hero. I didn’t have to know who wrote which pov. Silas had Colleen written all over him. He was perfect. Sweet, funny and adorable. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “I want to feel that again. I want to remember what it feels like to love someone like that. And not just anyone. I want to know what it feels like to love Charlie.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/da02ca9c-217c-4c72-963b-4f411232e8cd_zps963b310c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421229084i/13343584.jpg" alt=" photo da02ca9c-217c-4c72-963b-4f411232e8cd_zps963b310c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then there is Charlie. Once again, it didn’t surprise me that Tarryn wrote her. She has that snarky kind of humor that Tarryn does so well. <br><b>
  <blockquote>My drawers are neat. I must have OCD. I toss around the socks and underwear to see if I can piss myself off.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><i>Never Never</i> was a short book, and once I start reading I couldn’t put it down. The end left me with more questions than I had in the beginning and the second book can’t come soon enough! I’m glad I read it, but the waiting is going to be brutal. I know I’ll have to do a re-read before the next book is out! I'm going to leave this review short and sweet. It's one of those stories you just hate to read yourself!<br><br>Overall, if you’re looking for a well written and unique story that’s fast paced, mysterious and an all around intriguing read, pick this one up! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“We were an us, Charlie. And holy shit, I can see why.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/ba52f8c3-ae1a-4bfe-9066-adde3b00ec29_zps945866f1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421229222i/13343593.jpg" alt=" photo ba52f8c3-ae1a-4bfe-9066-adde3b00ec29_zps945866f1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4880366020746423195" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1082288479" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1082288479" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1082288479?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/28933326-never-never">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=childhood-loves">childhood-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=wtf-did-i-just-read">wtf-did-i-just-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1082288479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17387631376436275608">Please see more of my reviews at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.bookaddicthaven.com'>www.bookaddicthaven.com</a> <br/><br/>I didn't expect to like this serial as much as I did. I had seen plenty of bad reviews for this series, but I am always looking for quick audiobooks that I can finish between other, "deeper" audiobook selections. 'Never Never' was exactly the type of quick, "filler" audiobook that I was looking for.<br/><br/>Admittedly, I was wrong about this story. I was completely captivated by this story right from the start. It was just so different from everyth</span>
  <span id="freeText17387631376436275608" style="display:none">Please see more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a> <br /><br />I didn't expect to like this serial as much as I did. I had seen plenty of bad reviews for this series, but I am always looking for quick audiobooks that I can finish between other, "deeper" audiobook selections. 'Never Never' was exactly the type of quick, "filler" audiobook that I was looking for.<br /><br />Admittedly, I was wrong about this story. I was completely captivated by this story right from the start. It was just so different from everything else I'd read. I ended up reading all three books back to back, because I couldn't pull myself away until I knew what happened.<br /><br />The story is centered on two high school sweethearts, Charlie and Silas. It is immediately apparent that Charlie has some sort of unexplained memory loss. She can't remember her name or anything about her life. She is scared, but decides to go through the motions at school until she can piece her missing memories back together.<br /><br />Charlie walks through her school day, doing her best to soak up every detail. She does her best to change her behavior in response to the reactions of her "friends", slowly identifying her usual behaviors and preferences. She is introduced to her boyfriend, Silas, but has no recollection of him either.<br /><br />After spending the day together, Charlie figures out that she isn't the only one faking it. It is clear that Silas has absolutely no idea of who she is either. Things go from strange to outright bizarre! <br /><br />Circumstances throw these two virtual strangers together. They form a fast alliance, working together to try and figure out what is going on with them. Despite growing closer to one another, all the clues that they unearth paint a disturbing picture. <br /><br />They were not the happy couple that everyone thought. Both of them had secrets...big ones! Now, they risk losing their newfound happiness as they come to terms with their betrayals.<br /><br />Emotions run high and tempers flare. Like most YA stories, there is plenty of angst and back &amp; forth to hold your attention. There is no shortage of teenage drama here.<br /><br />That being said, you need to be in the mood for this kind of story. On another day, I might have found the exact same story to be immature and irritating. However, it was exactly what I was in the mood for at the time. <br /><br />The first of three serials, this book ends with a huge cliffhanger. That shouldn't be a surprise. If you're like me, you'll want to finish the series immediately. <br /><br />This story was highly unbelievable, but greatly entertaining. It's one of those books where you're thinking, "Yeah right" and rolling your eyes...but you can't stop listening anyway because you love every implausible minute. Yep, I was hooked! I started the second book immediately after finishing Part I.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17387631376436275608" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3252303624" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3252303624" />
    <a title="jessica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica"><img alt="jessica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1509983330p2/10171516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3252303624?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="jessica" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica">jessica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781506107158" href="/book/show/24509473-never-never">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3252303624" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6319271550095770355">author collaborations always make me nervous - especially when it involves an author i adore (hoover) and an author im not really a fan of (fisher). from past experience, one of three things can happen:<blockquote>- i like the book because i want to support the author i love,<br/><br/>- i dont enjoy the novel because it reminds why i dislike the other author to begin with, OR <br/><br/>- the story doesnt feel like it was written by either author and then im just confused. lol.</blockquote> with this story, im finding myself in the last sce</span>
  <span id="freeText6319271550095770355" style="display:none">author collaborations always make me nervous - especially when it involves an author i adore (hoover) and an author im not really a fan of (fisher). from past experience, one of three things can happen:<blockquote>- i like the book because i want to support the author i love,<br /><br />- i dont enjoy the novel because it reminds why i dislike the other author to begin with, OR <br /><br />- the story doesnt feel like it was written by either author and then im just confused. lol.</blockquote> with this story, im finding myself in the last scenario. im confused, i have no idea what either author was thinking when they wrote this or why they both approved of it (especially part three), but wow. this is pretty <i>meh</i>. not great, not horrible. just pretty mediocre. and i have a hard time believing either author is okay with mediocrity. <br /><br />as a whole, the concept is pretty unique. i enjoy how this first and second parts really engage in the mystery aspect of the story and sets up the plot and characters in a way that makes me want to root for them and discover what is happening. but part three completely ruins the story. it really made me realise that world building is nonexistent and the story is highly underdeveloped in many ways. it seriously made me question why i enjoyed the first two parts. and what even was that epilogue!?! <br /><br />this mini-series is proof that sometimes authors have brain farts and its not <i>always</i> a good idea to publish every story well-established authors write. <br /><br /><b>part one ↠ <i>3.5 stars</i></b><br /><b>part two ↠ <i>3.5 stars</i></b><br /><b>part three ↠ <i>2.5 stars</i></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6319271550095770355" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13163730629472540884"><b>3.5 STARS! ★★★☆</b><br/><br/>Well this book was one whole gigantic tease of a mystery with almost zero answers given to us. <br/><br/><b>Me after reading the first chapter:</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420864412ra/13281003.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Me after reading the last page:</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420864412ra/13281003.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And let it be known that there is this <b>HUGE cliffy at the end</b> of this one that can rival against that cliffy in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23312692.Nocte__The_Nocte_Trilogy___1_' title='Nocte (The Nocte Trilogy, #1) by Courtney Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Nocte</a> <-- yeah remember THAT gigantic cliffy where you'd want to hunt down the author and hold her at gunpoint to reveal the answers we need?! <br/><br/>I liked that the concept is unique and original, plus I expected noth</span>
  <span id="freeText13163730629472540884" style="display:none"><b>3.5 STARS! ★★★☆</b><br><br>Well this book was one whole gigantic tease of a mystery with almost zero answers given to us. <br><br><b>Me after reading the first chapter:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420864412ra/13281003.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Me after reading the last page:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420864412ra/13281003.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And let it be known that there is this <b>HUGE cliffy at the end</b> of this one that can rival against that cliffy in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23312692.Nocte__The_Nocte_Trilogy___1_" title="Nocte (The Nocte Trilogy, #1) by Courtney Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Nocte</a> &lt;-- yeah remember THAT gigantic cliffy where you'd want to hunt down the author and hold her at gunpoint to reveal the answers we need?! <br><br>I liked that the concept is unique and original, plus I expected nothing less when it involves these two brilliant authors. Imagine Tarryn's twisted ideas thrown in with CoHo's signature hero that you'd like to take home for Sunday brunches with your family. And BAM! You'll get this little brainchild that comes in the form of an unconventional love story shrouded in mystery but also sprinkled with some adorable humor and yummy grilled cheese (that's all on you, CoHo). <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420865196ra/13281145.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All I can say so far that it's like a mix of second chance romance where the MCs get to start off with a clean slate again or reading a romance story backwards since they were lovers prior to them suffering a bad case of amnesia (or so it seems). We get to see them slowly discovering things about their past <b>but at this point, Charlie &amp; Silas are as clueless as us readers are.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/616053.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My only issue would be wishing that the authors would have waited to release this as a standalone novel rather than a 140-pages novella at this point. This book seemed to have only scratched the surface of what could have been a potentially amazing read had it been a standalone. Had I known that it was this short and ends with a huge cliffy with no official news on the next release date, I would have held it off. But alas, my relationship with CoHo's books seemed to get the better of me. <br><br>Overall, it's different and it's not a read that you can just box it into a particular category. It has a little bit of everything and possibly more; it captivates you yet it confuses you. Definitely a page-turner but if you're not a fan of cliffhangers, I'd highly advise you to wait till the next book is out before picking this one up. <br><br><i>PS: My theory so far, if anyone is interested. </i><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Definitely running along the lines of PNR or more precisely, a case of voodoo or black magic going on. New Orleans have been known famous for these stuffs, so can't say it's a mere coincidence that the authors chose the story to be taking place there. Char/Si could have pissed someone off so badly (maybe Shrimp Girl, who knows? Or maybe she knows how to help them or sth) that they got hit with this "curse". OR MAYBE they inflicted these on themselves. Maybe they wanted a chance to start afresh, wipe off their bad traits.<br><br>GAH WHO KNOWS?! Damnit now I really need the next book! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1161179741?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1161179741" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9390630462101065813"><b> 3 stars! </b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/noidea.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420782578i/13261714.png' alt=' photo noidea.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>First off I'd like to reiterate that <b> just because I rate a book 3 stars doesn't mean it wasn't good. </b> It just means I didn't love it. I liked this book, I did. I just wish I had waited to read this until the 2nd book was released. Because this book ends on a <b> CLIFFHANGER!!!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>I don't want to give anything away, so in the tradition of the lovely <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/21830787-kat-stark' rel='nofollow noopener'> Kat Stark </a>, this is my (mini) unconventional review.<br/><br/><b> My thoughts while I was reading this book: </b><br/><br/>-"Hmm, Tarryn Fisher really has a thin</span>
  <span id="freeText9390630462101065813" style="display:none"><b> 3 stars! </b> <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/noidea.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420782578i/13261714.png" alt=" photo noidea.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>First off I'd like to reiterate that <b> just because I rate a book 3 stars doesn't mean it wasn't good. </b> It just means I didn't love it. I liked this book, I did. I just wish I had waited to read this until the 2nd book was released. Because this book ends on a <b> CLIFFHANGER!!!!!!!!</b><br><br>I don't want to give anything away, so in the tradition of the lovely <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/21830787-kat-stark" rel="nofollow noopener"> Kat Stark </a>, this is my (mini) unconventional review.<br><br><b> My thoughts while I was reading this book: </b><br><br>-"Hmm, Tarryn Fisher really has a thing for amnesia."<br><br>-"Damn, this book reminds me a lot of Don't Look Back by Jennifer Armentrout just with 2 people and not 1 person."<br><br>-"OMG CoHo soooooooooooo wrote that part."<br><br>-"Why are they so focused on kissing each other rather than figuring out what's happening to them? Those are some damn strong horny hormones!"<br><br>-"Now I want a grilled cheese. Damn it, that was CoHo's doing again!"<br><br>-"Eeek! A penis!"<br><br><br>I will say that despite there being a cliffy (which I expected) it was a DAMN GOOD cliffy.<br><br>So overall, I like the concept but I wish this book had been more than 140 pages. I will read book 2. Whenever it decides to come along.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9390630462101065813" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

And before anyone goes all Sassy Troll on me, I’mma beat you to the punch and say <b>NOPE – IT’S NOT A NOVELLA EITHER</b>. It is a third of a book. It’s the equivalent of going to your local bookstore, picking a 300 page book off the shelf, ripping the first 100 or so pages out, reading only that portion of the story, and having the clerk tell you the next 100 pages won't be available for you to read for another 5 months . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/texas/houston/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>What it was instead? Well, I don’t even fucking know since the story never went ANYWHERE in the 118 pages provided on my Nook version. In order to prevent mass spoilage, I'll just say all you ever really know is Silas and Charlie “wake up” with no memories. <br><br>Silas was your typical New Adult male MC. You know, the kind all the girls will be dropping their panties for all over the interwebs. Kinda like this guy . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/texas/houston/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430837384ra/14767742.gif" alt="Houston commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Unless you’re <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/2644090-erica" rel="nofollow noopener">Erica</a>.   <a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/texas/houston/" rel="nofollow noopener">

  </a>

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430837384ra/14767744.gif" alt="Houston commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>(Why do men get such a bad rap for writing terrible female characters? Female writers are just as bad.)<br><br>The rest of the “book” was spent . . . well, kinda doing nothing. And that ending????<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/texas/houston/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430837384ra/14767745.gif" alt="Houston commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That’s not to say <i>Never Never</i> can’t end up being decent by the time it’s all done. This should have served as a lesson that publication dates/pre-orders shouldn’t be accepted before an author (or in this case, authors) is anywhere close to being finished with a story. Calling it a “series” when it’s obviously a stand-alone novel broken into three sections is more than a bit shady. Not to mention all the superfans (many who are young girls spending their <b>allowance</b>) who will be dropping THREE TIMES the price they normally do in order to read what is really one book . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/texas/houston/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer3066709900306188538">**Before reading**<br/><br/><b>WHAT??? COLLEEN HOOVER AND TARRYN FISHER WILL WRITE A BOOK? <br/>TOGETHER???? <br/>I CAN'T.... *jumps up and down*<br/><br/>Best news ever!</b><br/><br/>**After reading**<br/><br/>So...<br/>What the hell was that? <br/>First of all, it should have been announced that this would be a serial novel and not series or standalone.<br/>Second, this premise is nothing new or original or special or that shocking.   <span id="freeText3066709900306188538" style="display:none">**Before reading**<br /><br /><b>WHAT??? COLLEEN HOOVER AND TARRYN FISHER WILL WRITE A BOOK? <br />TOGETHER???? <br />I CAN'T.... *jumps up and down*<br /><br />Best news ever!</b><br /><br />**After reading**<br /><br />So...<br />What the hell was that? <br />First of all, it should have been announced that this would be a serial novel and not series or standalone.<br />Second, this premise is nothing new or original or special or that shocking. Obviously, other's people definition of mind fuck is different from mine. <br />Third, so many things that are just... stupid! Okay, they don't remember anything. Two pages later - they do remember some things. Oh, how convenient! Hey, our lives are turned upside down by some unexplainable event - but they act like they are out on the first date or some shit like that. A lot of pathetic love scenes. In the story with a premise that DOESN'T NEED THOSE! <br />Fourth, I got a feeling that this whole thing was written because both authors knew it would bring them a lot of attention and possibly money and high sales rank. <br /><br />I'm disappointed and I need break from both CoHo and Tarryn Fisher because I'm just annoyed now. </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claudia Ramírez" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claudia Ramírez" href="/user/show/13061577-claudia-ram-rez">Claudia Ramírez</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13061577-claudia-ram-rez?shelf=i-ship-them">i-ship-them</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081812539" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17440147395410903736">I'm only giving this 4 stars because it was TOO short to feel like an actual book! I really think this would had worked PERFECTLY as a standalone! But aside from that, I FREAKING LOVED IT! The characters were awesome, specially Silas, I'm in love with him already. Also Landon, he's a sweetheart <3. <br/><br/>I'm really interested in what will happen next! The things we found out in the first book left me with my mouth hanging open! What's up with that Brian and Avril?! Ughhh, I want to slap Silas and Char</span>
  <span id="freeText17440147395410903736" style="display:none">I'm only giving this 4 stars because it was TOO short to feel like an actual book! I really think this would had worked PERFECTLY as a standalone! But aside from that, I FREAKING LOVED IT! The characters were awesome, specially Silas, I'm in love with him already. Also Landon, he's a sweetheart &lt;3. <br /><br />I'm really interested in what will happen next! The things we found out in the first book left me with my mouth hanging open! What's up with that Brian and Avril?! Ughhh, I want to slap Silas and Charlie, I want to know why they did those horrible things! I also want to know what's causing their memory loss! The ending left us with a big cliffhanger and I almost cried! I don't know why! I think it's because I was able to put myself in the place of the main characters and I felt what Silas was feeling in that moment with the letters, I was so confused and worried and with a hole in my heart! <br /><br />Now I can't wait to read the second part, and the cover just freaks me out! Where is the other hand?! Why is it tinted with red?! I hope we get a Colleenesque ending to these books, because if they went with Tarryn's way, I'M EXPECTING THE WORST! <br /><br />Stupid, stupid cliffhanger.<br />But AWESOME, awesome book! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17440147395410903736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1081803454" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1081803454" />
    <a title="Vilma Iris" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15777655-vilma-iris"><img alt="Vilma Iris" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1501855386p2/15777655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081803454?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vilma Iris" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vilma Iris" href="/user/show/15777655-vilma-iris">Vilma Iris</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081803454" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1250568374609889839"><b>A chilling, captivating thriller.</b><br/>Hoover and Fisher have combined their unique talents to deliver a deliciously twisted tale of deceit, love and friendship that keeps you guessing long after the heart-stopping end.<br/><br/>Check your preconceptions at the door, readers. This is a different—and exciting—Colleen Hoover/Tarryn Fisher experience. Never Never is a story that defies a specific category. It’s romantic, suspenseful, witty, edgy, mysterious and even creepy. I loved it!!! It has a supernatural twis</span>
  <span id="freeText1250568374609889839" style="display:none"><b>A chilling, captivating thriller.</b><br>Hoover and Fisher have combined their unique talents to deliver a deliciously twisted tale of deceit, love and friendship that keeps you guessing long after the heart-stopping end.<br><br>Check your preconceptions at the door, readers. This is a different—and exciting—Colleen Hoover/Tarryn Fisher experience. Never Never is a story that defies a specific category. It’s romantic, suspenseful, witty, edgy, mysterious and even creepy. I loved it!!! It has a supernatural twist that fuels the intriguing crux of the novel, sparking endless possibilities to conjure in one’s mind. Chapters alternate protagonist point-of-views as we piece together what’s happening in a book that starts with a blank.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“How odd to be made of flesh, balanced on bone, and filled with a soul you’ve never met.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Charlie and Silas have been friends since they were young, together since they were teenagers and now they’re strangers.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I look at her, she’s the girl I supposedly make love to. The girl I’ve apparently made love to for a while. The girl I apparently still love. I just wish I could remember …”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The book’s mysterious circumstances begin to unveil, as Silas and Charlie’s story takes shape. The plot-driven approach peppers fragments of who they are slowly, as they react to situations and each other. I won’t divulge too much information, as it’s best to experience this story blindly, but I’ll share that their tale is twisted and unusual. Not only that, there are shocking truths that change everything, and nothing is at it seems. And these truths… they’re mere glimpses of what’s to come and it makes the story feel more sinister.<br><br>The story moves quickly and concludes with a totally heart-stopping, leave-me-breathless, oh-my-godding kind of ending. It was brilliant and it totally rocked. I promise that like me, you’ll be more than ready to devour the next book in this compelling new series. Ready to unravel this mystery to the core. Ready to embrace what is sure to be more chilling… more thrilling… more spellbinding.<br><br>Overall, it was a wonderfully suspenseful, addictive book. I was happy to see these two differently styled authors come together to push the boundaries of their individual comfort zones, and the result is definitely something to gush over. They’ve given us a page turner of a story we are sure to remember.<br><br><b>He’ll do anything to remember.<br>She’ll do anything to forget.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413488677i/11519354._SY540_.jpg" width="462.4" height="462.4" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>✦ ✦ ✦ ✦<br><br><b> Follow Vilma's Book Blog: </b> <a href="http://vilmasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Website</a> | <a href="www.facebook.com/vilmasbookblog" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/vilmasbookblog" rel="nofollow noopener"> Twitter </a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1250568374609889839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1158833865" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1158833865" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1158833865?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=overrated-books">overrated-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1158833865" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9150919950277393571"><br/>Despite some issues I have with the book, I must say that this is a very unique and intriguing read and I really enjoyed most of it.<br/> <br/>The story to me is a first and I find it really very clever of the authors to create a story (in less 159 pages) of teaching two people who clearly love each other but who keep messing around and taking for granted what they have the hardest way to learn their lesson.<br/> <br/>Come to think of it, it does follow the fairy tale formula. A mean, uncaring girl and a stuck up, </span>
  <span id="freeText9150919950277393571" style="display:none"><br>Despite some issues I have with the book, I must say that this is a very unique and intriguing read and I really enjoyed most of it.<br> <br>The story to me is a first and I find it really very clever of the authors to create a story (in less 159 pages) of teaching two people who clearly love each other but who keep messing around and taking for granted what they have the hardest way to learn their lesson.<br> <br>Come to think of it, it does follow the fairy tale formula. A mean, uncaring girl and a stuck up, popular dude in a too perfect relationship- THEY NEEDED TO RUIN IT. So one day, a paranormal force perhaps a curse? intervenes to make them forget completely who they are. I have a strong feeling Tarryn Fisher has a lot do with the amnesia ingredient.^^<br> <br>As the MCs try to solve the mystery of their characters, they learn about the not so good side of their selves. This mystery is like the second chance to be better people than they used to be or so I hope would be the direction of the story.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430263429ra/14699187.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>I find it very amusing when the characters were trying to resolve the mystery to their situation by referring to popular fairytales. <br> <br>My main problem is such a story would have been so much more appropriate if the MCs weren’t in high school. It greatly bothered me that cheating and sleeping around <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ with the guidance counselor, no less! MY GOODNESS!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> would be ordinary occurrences. I think this is the main thing that ruined the story- the choice of characters.<br> <br>I wasn’t really that surprised at the cliffy because I expected there was going to be a major one, thanks to spoilers. But it still managed to give me Goosebumps.<br> <br>The premise is great.<br>The characters are inappropriate. <br>The writing isn’t very special but it was amusing and easy to read.<br>The plot is not very satisfying which makes me want to read the sequel even more!<br> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9150919950277393571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1081847924" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1081847924" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081847924?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081847924" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13434458628333866194"><b>4.5 Stars</b> ~ <b>
  <i>”What does Never Never mean?”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span> <br/><br/>Colleen Hoover and Tarryn Fisher collaborated on this book/series with a mysterious storyline of two high school teens who wake up in history class without a clue of who/where they are and why they have lost their memories.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>”I’m starting to not like who we are, Silas. You’re a rich kid who’s a dick to your housekeeper. I’m a mean teenager with absolutely no personality who takes selfies to make herself feel more important.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>As the stor</span>
  <span id="freeText13434458628333866194" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b> ~ <b>
  <i>”What does Never Never mean?”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>Colleen Hoover and Tarryn Fisher collaborated on this book/series with a mysterious storyline of two high school teens who wake up in history class without a clue of who/where they are and why they have lost their memories.<br><br><b>
  <i>”I’m starting to not like who we are, Silas. You’re a rich kid who’s a dick to your housekeeper. I’m a mean teenager with absolutely no personality who takes selfies to make herself feel more important.”</i>
</b><br><br>As the story progresses through dual povs of Charlie and Silas we find that they have been long time family friends, boyfriend/girlfriend with one another for most their lives and their families are connected. <br><br><b>
  <i>”We were an us, Charlie. And holy shit, I can see why.”</i>
</b><br><br>The writing was what a reader would expect from these wonderful authors… just excellent as were all characters presented. The more the two find out about themselves the more questions come with each discovery. <br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>To my disappointment this is a pretty short story that left me still not sure where the story is going and what the future holds for Silas and Charlie. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492491362ra/22521621.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>My stalking ventures have already commenced but so far I haven’t seen any teasers yet for the second and final book of this series. Oh I also totally guessed which author wrote which character I think friends will easily appreciate both author’s touches and join me in counting down the days till May 18th!! <br><br><b>
  <i>”Never stop. Never forget.”</i>
</b><br></span>

    <a title=". (not active on this account stop adding me)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29601169-not-active-on-this-account-stop-adding-me"><img alt=". (not active on this account stop adding me)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1566458755p2/29601169.jpg" /></a>

<div id="review_1081910799" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1081910799" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081910799?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081910799" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14032345600067532999">This book is one tasty mindf*ck and I loved every minute of it. How could I not? I love both authors...one's a little naughty and one's a little nice. Mix them together and <b>BAM</b>...this is what you get! <br/><br/>I could literally do this gif over and over...and over! Every time I thought I had something figured out, nope - see gif! ;) <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298466ra/684232.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>One thing I must mention is that the flow is so seamless! I really tried to pay attention and see if I could figure out who was writing what but I just got too wrapped up in </span>
  <span id="freeText14032345600067532999" style="display:none">This book is one tasty mindf*ck and I loved every minute of it. How could I not? I love both authors...one's a little naughty and one's a little nice. Mix them together and <b>BAM</b>...this is what you get! <br><br>I could literally do this gif over and over...and over! Every time I thought I had something figured out, nope - see gif! ;) <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298466ra/684232.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One thing I must mention is that the flow is so seamless! I really tried to pay attention and see if I could figure out who was writing what but I just got too wrapped up in the story...for the most part. There were times I was certain this had to be TF and other times, it had to be CoHo but in the end, it didn't really matter because it just worked. <br><br>So the story...starts off with Charlie not being able to remember a thing about herself...right in the middle of the day! It wasn't like she woke up and couldn't remember anything. Nope, she was just going along her day and drew a blank...at school. (Almost like those dreams you have where you can't remember where your classes are and you're having a big test? Yeah, like that.) Luckily, she's in the same class with Silas who's going through the <i>exact same thing</i> and of course, he's her boyfriend. <br><br>They try to figure out their lives and they get some answers rather quickly but then almost as many questions. Their families were close and something happened and now they hate each other. Silas and Charlie aren't suppose to be together but it's kind of hard to do when you've been with someone for four years...happily <i>or not</i>. (But the tattoos? LOVED that!) <br><br>There's not really any steaminess...a little romance and a juicy kiss though. Oh and lots of goose bumps! ;) <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421137348ra/13327727.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thankfully, we get both their POVs. It was interesting to see their feelings come out and how they reacted to things in the past.<br><br><b>Question everything</b>....or just go with the flow. Either way, you're not gonna be able to figure this puppy out. I actually had some ideas but the ending threw all those out the window. <br><br>The one thing I know for sure...I would take Silas as a boyfriend any day...memory or not. He is that yummy! <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421118675i/13324905.jpg" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ <b>
  <i>"Never stop. Never forget.</i>
</b><br><br>♥ “I don’t know myself well, but I can tell I have a lot of game.”<br><br>♥ "I’m Tetris Silas. All my pieces and parts are going to fit into all of your pieces and parts.”<br><br>♥ “Are we…are we about to make out? Because I didn’t picture it going down like this.”<br><br>♥ “We’re branded. You and me. We are so in <i>love</i>, Charlie. You feeling it yet? Do I make your heart go pitter patter?”<br> <br>♥ “I don’t care what our real first kiss was,” he says. “That’s the one I want to remember.”<br><br>♥ “We were an us, Charlie. And holy shit, I can see why.”<br><br><br><br>♦ BR w/Melissa! <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14032345600067532999" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <b>6 STARS</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Genre:</b> YA/NA Crossover – romance & mystery.<br/><b>Cover:</b> 9/10 <br/><b>Writing:</b> 10/10<br/><b>Heroine:</b> 8/10<br/><b>Hero:</b> 10/10<br/><b>Humour:</b> 5/10<br/><b>Hotness:</b> 2/10<br/><b>Romance:</b> 8/10<br/><b>Extra book Details:</b> Heroine & Hero POV; 1st person.
