I wouldn't change a thing. And I want to read it all over again already.</b><br/><br/>- - - - - - -Very mild spoilers for the book blurb ah</span>
  <span id="freeText14364811302924612885" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420805971ra/13268227.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>6 STARS</b>
</blockquote><br><b>Genre:</b> YA/NA Crossover – romance &amp; mystery.<br><b>Cover:</b> 9/10 <br><b>Writing:</b> 10/10<br><b>Heroine:</b> 8/10<br><b>Hero:</b> 10/10<br><b>Humour:</b> 5/10<br><b>Hotness:</b> 2/10<br><b>Romance:</b> 8/10<br><b>Extra book Details:</b> Heroine &amp; Hero POV; 1st person. Approx 150 Kindle pages. Not a stand-alone.<br><br><b>6 stars because... I couldn't put it down. I laughed. I loved the story, the writing, the mystery, the romance, the plot, the characters. I wouldn't change a thing. And I want to read it all over again already.</b><br><br>- - - - - - -Very mild spoilers for the book blurb ahead- - - - - - -<br><br><i>Never Never</i> is about 18 year old Silas &amp; 17 year old Charlie, forgetting who they are &amp; everyone else in the process, in the middle of a school day.<br><br>What ensues is all about them finding out who they were in their 'past lives' and trying to find clues to the mystery of their missing memories. Ultimately getting to know each other all over again. They don't feel like themselves at all, but all they know is they only have each other.<br><br>- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -<br><br><b>I know I said I was going to wait for the reviews to appear. But I couldn't resist seeing what Fisher &amp; Hoover hand in store for me. And I'm very grateful I didn't wait. I loved going in blind.<br><br>All I can say is that I loved this book. Silas was awesome, funny, romantic, clever. Charlie I felt for, I also admired her. The mystery &amp; plot was totally surprising and unique. And I am just DYING for the next book.</b><br><br>- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -<br><br>As promised, for my friends who are worried about cheating:<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ok so, first and foremost, yes they both cheat on each other. We haven't got a clue why. And there is no description of this cheating whatsoever; what I mean is we don't experience it first hand. The two characters that they cheat with are in it briefly, the girl Silas cheated with is in it VERY briefly. They both find out that they were cheaters when their 'cheating partners' come onto them.<br><br>But it is highly stressed that the 'present' Silas &amp; Charlie are very different to who they were in their 'past life'. They both despise that they cheated. Silas comes across as more emotional about it, he hates the guy Charlie cheated with instantly, and he's much more remorseful over his cheating. He is disgusted with himself and is already starting to love Charlie, he can't believe he would ever do such a thing. Charlie almost feels relieved that she wasn't the only one to cheat, she has been hating who she discovers she was.<br><br>All in all, it's a very small part of the story, there's no description and it's very brief. It's probably only included so that, by the end of the story, there is some kind of transformation from the not so nice people they were and the amazing people they are now. That their love was tested and that their memory loss was the best thing that could have happened because it brought them closer together. At least I hope so :D <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407252752i/10663054.jpg" alt="" height="110" width="210" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Like I said, I have a Love/Hate relationship with serials. I hate them because of the cliffys, but I love them because of the cliffys. <br><br>I know. I’m a little crazy.<br><br>I really DID LIKE Never Never as a serial. I felt like if it was any longer I would have gotten bored with the storyline and needed a break. The pace was fast and slow at the same time.<br><br>It’s about the Hero and Heroine not having any memories. They do not know who they are and why they both lost their memories.<br><br>It was fast because <b>I HAD NO CLUE TO WHAT WAS GOING ON</b>, it was kind of slow because the characters had no clue to what was going on and as they were putting the pieces together, I felt like it just needed the pace to pick up (JUST A TINY BIT). <br><br>Anyhow, if you are like me and was a bit hesitant because you didn’t like Ugly Love, or The Opportunist, well you will not be disappointed with Never Never.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24378015.Never_Never__Never_Never___1_" title="Never Never (Never Never, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText71696260090643316" style="display:none">★ /5<br />This is a short book without anything good in it.<br /><br />As a person who didn‘t know anything about the plot, I was a very confused and bored entire book. As the story went further and further I welt more and more detached from the story. Honestly, nothing meaningful happened until the very end.<br /><br />The book mainly focuses on the relationship between Charlie and Silas, two teenagers as they are trying to regain their lost memory. They as characters for me were unbearable to follow because I didn‘t like any aspect of their relationship to others and themselves, their personalities felt very basic and they had a lot of unnecessary characteristics witch didn't help their character arcs.<br /><br />Personally, I'm not the biggest fan of this novel. It is very short and practically nothing happens.<br /></span>

<div id="review_1082203074" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1082203074" />
    <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review"><img alt="Peek At My Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1414761368p2/18263404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1082203074?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Peek At My Book Review" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review">Peek At My Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1082203074" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3678105599701172353"><b>3 ‘WTF Just Happened’ Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421218112i/13341855._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>My Review :</b> Okay, since this for me <b> wasn’t a complete story </b> just part of it, this review won’t do justice the book but I’ll try my best here. First this book was confusing beyond measures, more than 50% of the book is just Charlie’s and Silas’ daily routine except here they do not remember Person that’s present in their lives but they do remember other stuffs like celebrities, song’s lyrics, television show, passwords etc. Honestly for the first 50%b I didn’t enjoy i</span>
  <span id="freeText3678105599701172353" style="display:none"><b>3 ‘WTF Just Happened’ Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421218112i/13341855._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My Review :</b> Okay, since this for me <b> wasn’t a complete story </b> just part of it, this review won’t do justice the book but I’ll try my best here. First this book was confusing beyond measures, more than 50% of the book is just Charlie’s and Silas’ daily routine except here they do not remember Person that’s present in their lives but they do remember other stuffs like celebrities, song’s lyrics, television show, passwords etc. Honestly for the first 50%b I didn’t enjoy it, I know the authors kept all for the last BOOM but I cannot ignore the fact that I was bored to death with two people who are trying to remember their lives. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421218112i/13341856.jpg" width="400" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The next 50% was when I just couldn’t put the book down; we started to get some answers even though a bit vague and all those suspense. Since we were getting the book from Silas’s and Charlie’s pov we as readers were in the same boat as theirs, we were as <b> confused, in dilemma, frustrated </b> and wanted answers just as them…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421218112ra/13341857.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now we need answers from the next book, I’m hoping to be <b> aghast </b> by these two authors. <br><br><br>My theory about what happen in a fuzzy way.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[First concerning the cheating that Silas is sleeping with someone and Charlie is sleeping with another guy, I think that this was all a pretense because they needed to show that they were no longer on love because of their father’s rivalry. Because it is clear by the evidences that they found Silas and Charlie are deeply in love with each other, the only evidences which shows that they were cheating on each other are what other people are saying and not what they have as possessions for instance a picture, a letter etc. But I’m not very sure!!!<br><br>Then as for why do they forget, I have <b> two theories </b>…What!!!I’m on the same boat as you are so obviously I have many things going in my mind ;) First let consider the clues that we got from the first book. We have <b> Charlie’s Father, the business, and the shrimp</b>!!!<br>My first theory is that they went to a shrink for some reasons (maybe because of their father’s business which is an important clue here) and that is why they were brainwashed or something like that. But why I have No idea…<br>My last theory is that they took some kind of pills to make themselves forget or someone gave them something deliberately - but here also it has got something to do with their father’s business. <br>But what does that girl Shrimp knows and why is she so scared of Charlie???<br>Why was the lost file under Silas’ bed??? If he stole it, why he didn’t reveal anything even though Carlie’s father is in jail?<br>One more thing that I couldn’t understand why in the blurb it’s said “He'll do anything to remember. She'll do anything to forget”, for me both were trying to remember right?? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421240702i/13345440._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If these are not what is going to happen in the next then these two authors are <b> absolute geniuses </b>!!!<br><br>The next book is coming May 17…<b>SO FAR AWAY and WE Need Answers!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421218112ra/13341858.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://peekatmybookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="70" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418569189i/12827092._SX540_.jpg" width="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><a href="https://twitter.com/theVrsha" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="60" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418815952i/12909809.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1164569858" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1164569858" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1164569858?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1164569858" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15072193695522050258"><b>Never….never have I been more pissed!!</b><br/><br/>You would think that for once, just once, Colleen Hoover or Tarryn Fisher could write something mediocre, something blah. They could manage to suck at least one time. Once! <br/><br/>Nope.<br/><br/>Their talent is effortless.<br/><br/>When I found out they were teaming up for <i>Never Never</i>, I thought there was a chance that their ferocious ability to write would cancel each other out. A cock fight of talent that would innately void the other’s writing. I was preparing for a mess. Either th</span>
  <span id="freeText15072193695522050258" style="display:none"><b>Never….never have I been more pissed!!</b><br /><br />You would think that for once, just once, Colleen Hoover or Tarryn Fisher could write something mediocre, something blah. They could manage to suck at least one time. Once! <br /><br />Nope.<br /><br />Their talent is effortless.<br /><br />When I found out they were teaming up for <i>Never Never</i>, I thought there was a chance that their ferocious ability to write would cancel each other out. A cock fight of talent that would innately void the other’s writing. I was preparing for a mess. Either that or the apocalypse. <br /><br />I didn’t expect their talents to match each other word for word. Their differences to fit in perfect sync forming a fluent one of a kind experience. <br /><br />The insurmountable talent these ladies possess falls into the category of things I’ll never understand. Like, why is it that no matter how many times I pee before I get into the shower, as soon as I step in the shower, I have to pee again? How do red lights always know when I’m running late? Why won’t the 5th dentist just cave and say he recommends Colgate too, and why is Wal-Mart taking over the world?<br /><br />I don’t understand it, and I didn’t expect it. <br /><br />This book exceeded all expectations.<br /><br />Believe it or not, I started <i>Never Never</i> without any knowledge of the plot. I didn’t know it was a plus sized novella, or part of a series. The vagueness of this very review is to hopefully provide others with the same blind leap of faith. <br /><br />Here is what I can tell you. <br /><br /><i>Never Never</i> is a penetratingly unique and original story that will capture you from the very first paragraph. It is suspenseful and heart pounding. An experience that’s one of a kind. But what I loved most, the very most, is how it made me feel. <br /><br />This <i>is</i> a love story at its core. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"I don't care what our first real kiss was. That's the one I want to remember."</b>
</i><br /><br />There were certain scenes where the love was so achingly intense, but not in an obvious way. In a way that was made to be felt. I would literally experience a flutter in the very pit of my stomach during certain parts; it almost hurt. I spent half of the time with a knot in my stomach, and the other half trying to figure everything out. Thinking I had figured it out, only to be taken in a completely different direction.<br /><br />My advice is to hold on, the experience is quick. Keep in mind that the plot centers on time. You find out the limitations of why certain things couldn’t have been developed more, even at times I wished for the “more”, but consider the plot. Consider why the authors had to make it work at such a rapid pace.<br /><br />The creativity of what these authors have done blows me away. They have brought something unique to a literary world that is saturated with repetition. Once you start, you will not be able to stop, and in the end you will be pissed as hell that you have to wait for more.<br /><br />I cannot wait for more.<br /><br />READ ON!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15072193695522050258" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sfBFwJuQ+mHV8dzNnWcjQOFEHklYpTnRZvpCgdQHkcaL1iwSIM4zCXLaaKxqkimfNxv5gZYot7Y9hAQwGURjXA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tWxnz2pRJaVWHg60/AbzRsGgkbrbn3gbCx/vzKPudiePSg4d0Q/szfE1utUL8/mZF/92chUS9nxQYal9bq2EvQ==')})
  }
//]]>
